[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDuring an automated fuzzing session of the `CompressTarFuzzer` harness against the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApache Commons Compress codebase, the fuzzer triggered a high-severity security [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfinding: a `FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh` of type “Remote Code Execution.” The crash [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack trace indicates that untrusted archive data led to an unsafe Java [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeserialization path in `TarArchiveEntry`, potentially allowing an attacker to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstantiate arbitrary classes on the classpath.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue observed  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer fed a crafted TAR stream to the library. While parsing the TAR header,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe code invoked Java’s `[0m[1;35mObjectInputStream.readObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which in turn triggered [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer’s detection of uncontrolled class or object creation. This was reported as a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“Remote Code Execution” vulnerability by the Jazzer runtime.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Remote Code Execution via unsafe deserialization of bytes from an archive. [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mUntrusted data is directly passed to `ObjectInputStream`, allowing instantiation of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marbitrary classes.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations and findings  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception is raised by `[0m[1;35mjaz.Zer.readObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` after an invocation of [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mObjectInputStream.readObject[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Stack trace frames of interest:  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.updateName[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls into serialization routines.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.parseTarHeaderUnwrapped[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mparseTarHeader[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstruct new entry objects from raw header bytes.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – The vulnerability is surfaced inside `TarArchiveEntry.<init>[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` when [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreading the entry name.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer reproducer and crash input are captured in the generated files [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., `Crash_<…>.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, demonstrating a minimal terminating case.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to investigate  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `[0m[1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.tar.TarArchiveEntry.updateName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` – [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling of header bytes and any deserialization logic.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Serialization paths invoked by `[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.parseTarHeader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and its [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcallers.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Any use of `java.io.ObjectInputStream` or related serialization APIs within [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtar-format parsing code.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness entrypoint [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`CompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to understand [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhow input bytes flow into the parsing routines.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis assessment covers the end-to-end reproduction, classification of the issue as [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsafe deserialization leading to remote code execution, and pinpoints the relevant[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode paths for further security review.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
